Kepha bafulathela (benqaba) ngakho-ke sathumela kubona izikhukhula (amanzi) aphuma edamini futhi sabashintshela izivande zabo ezimbili zaba yizivande zabo ezimbili ezithela izithelo ezibabayo namatamariski (uhlobo lwesihlahla) kanye nezomlothi ezimbalwa
Ngalokho sabanika umvuzo ngenxa yokuthi babengabongi bengakholwa futhi asijezisi ngalendlela ngaphandle kwabangakholwa
Futhi senza phakathi kwabo kanye namadolobha esasiwabusisile ukuthi kube amadolobha abonakalayo kalula futhi sahlukanisa phakathi kwawo uhambo, sathi “hambani phakathi kwawo ebusuku nasemini niphephile”
Kepha bathi, “Nkosi yethu yenza amabanga amade ohambweni lethu futhi bayona bona imiphefumulo yabo sabe sesibenza ondabuzekwayo futhi sabadabula ukudabulwa okuphelele, ngempela kunezimpawu kulokho kubona bonke ababekezelayo ababongayo
Futhi u-Iblis (uSathane) wawuqinisekisa ngabo umcabango wakhe, ngakho-ke bamlandela ngaphandle kweqembu labakholwayo
Futhi (uSathane) akanalo igunya phezu kwabo kepha ukuze sazi ukuthi ngubani okholelwa empilweni ezayo kulowo osekungabazeni ngayo, futhi iNkosi yakho ingumlondolozi wazona zonke izinto
Ithi “bizani labo enanibenza (onkulunkulu) esikhundleni sikaMvelinqangi abanalutho ngisho nokuncane kakhulu emazulwini nasemhlabeni futhi abanaso isabelo kukona kokubili futhi akanaye umlekeleli phakathi kwabo”
Futhi ukuncengela akusizi kuyena ngaphandle kwalowo amvumelayo kuze kuthi uma ukwesaba kususiwe ezihliziyweni zabo bathi, “yathini iNkosi yenu bathi iqiniso futhi yona iphakeme yinkulu”
Ithi, “ngubani oninika isabelo esivela emazulwini nasemhlabeni na?” ithi, “nguMvelinqangi” futhi ngempela yithina noma yinina mhlawumbe abasekuholweni noma abasekudukeni okucacile
Ithi angeke nibuzwe ngecala lethu futhi angeke sibuzwe ngalokho enikwenzayo
Ithi, iNkosi yethu iyosiqoqela ndawomye bese iyehlulela phakathi kwethu ngeqiniso futhi yona ingumehluleli onolwazi
Ithi ngikhombiseni labo enanimenzela abahlanganyeli ngabo, lutho! kepha yena unguMvelinqangi uphakeme ngamandla unobuhlakani
Futhi asizange sikuthumele ngaphandle kokuba ngumlethi wezindaba ezimnandi nomxwayisi kubantu bonke, kepha iningi labantu alazi
Futhi bathi siyofika nini lesisithembiso uma kungukuthi nina niqinisile na
Ithi isinqumo senu esosuku eningeke nikwazi ukulihlehlisa ihora futhi eningeke nikwazi ukulisheshisa
Futhi labo abangakholwanga bathi, “asisoze sikholelwe kuleQur’an ngisho noma kulokho okungaphambilini kwayo”, futhi uma ungazibona izoni zimisiwe ngaphambili kweNkosi yazo, ezinye zazo ziphendukela kwezinye ngezwi (lokusola), labo ababenziwe buthakathaka bayothi kulabo ababeqhosha “ukube kwakungesingenxa yenu sasizoba ngabakholwayo”
Labo ababeqhosha bathi kulabo ababenziwe buthakathaka “ngakube yithina yini esanivimbela ekuholweni emva kokuba sekunifikele na? Qhabo nina naniyizoni”
Futhi labo ababenziwe buthakathaka bathi kulabo ababeqhosha “kepha kwakuyisu lenu lasebusuku nasemini ngenkathi nisiphoqa ukuthi singakholwa kuMvelinqangi nokuthi simbekele izimbangi” futhi bayokufihla ukuzisola uma sebesibona isijeziso futhi siyowagaxa amaketango ezintamweni zalabo abangakholwanga, ngakube bayonikwa umvuzo ngaphandle kwalokho ababekwenza na
Futhi sasingakaze simthumele umxwayisi edolobheni ngaphandle kokuthi abanothile balo bathi, “ngempela asikholelwa kulokho enithunywe ngako”
Futhi bathi, “thina sinengcebo eningi kakhulu kanye nezingane futhi thina angeke sijeziswe
Ithi ngempela iNkosi yami iyasandisa isabelo kulowo emthandayo futhi isinciphiso kepha iningi labantu alazi
Futhi akusiyona ingcebo yenu noma izingane zenu ezinisondeza eduzane nathi kepha yilabo abakholwayo futhi abenza imisebenzi emihle elungileyo labo-ke okwabo umvuzo ophindiwe kabili ngenxa yalokho ababekwenza futhi bayohlala ezindaweni zokuhlala bephephile
Futhi labo abazabalazayo ukuphikisana namavesi ethu ukuwadikibalisa labo-ke bayolethwa esijezisweni
Ithi ngempela iNkosi yami iyaselula isabelo kunoma ngabe ngubani eyimthandayo ezincekwini zayo futhi imnciphisele futhi noma ngabe yini oluthize enilusebenzisayo (eninikela ngalo) ngakho-ke yona iyolubuyisa futhi yona ingcono kunabobonke abanika isabelo”
Futhi ngosuku eyobaqoqela ngalo ndawonye bonke bese ithi ezingelosini, “ngakube yibona yini laba ababenikhonza na?”
(Izingelosi) ziyothi, “udumo malube kuwe! wena ungumvikeli wethu hhayi bona, kepha babekhonza amaJinn, abaningi babo babengabakholelwa kuwona”
Ngakho-ke ngalolusuku abekho abanye benu abaphathela abanye inzuzo nokulimala futhi siyothi kulabo abona, “yizwani isijeziso somlilo leso enanisiphika”
Futhi uma befundelwa amavesi ethu acacile bathi, “lona akayilutho ngaphandle kokuba yindoda eyithanda ukunivimbela kulokho okwakukhonzwa ngoyihlo”, futhi bathi “lokhu akuyilutho ngaphandle kwamanga aqanjiwe futhi bathi labo abazange bakholwe mayelana neqiniso ngenkathi lifika kubona “lokhu akuyilutho ngaphandle komlingo ocacile”
Futhi asibanikezanga izincwadi ababengazifunda futhi asizange simthumele kubona umxwayisi ngaphambilini kwakho
Nalabo ababengaphambilini kwabo baliphika (iqiniso) futhi laba abakayitholi ngisho ingxenye eyodwa eshumini yaloko esabanika kona (abasendulo) kepha baziphika izithunywa zami ngakho-ke kwakunjani ukuphika kwami
Ithi kuphela nginelulekela entweni eyodwa ukuthi niphakamele uMvelinqangi ngababili nangamunye bese niyacabanga ukuthi benikanye naye akukho ukuhlanya kuye, akayilutho ngaphandle kokuba ngumxwayisi wenu ngaphambi kwesijeziso esinzima
Ithi noma ngabe yimuphi umvuzo, engiwucela kunina ungowenu, umvuzo wami ukuMvelinqangi kuphela futhi yena ungufakazi phezu kwezinto zonke
Ithi ngempela iNkosi yami iyaliveza iqiniso, isazi sokungabonwayo
Ithi iqiniso selifikile futhi inkohliso angeke isungulwe futhi angeke iphindwe
Ithiumangiphambukakuphelangiphambukelaumphefumulo wami futhi uma ngiholiwe kungenxa yalokho iNkosi yami ekwembulile kumina ngempela yona iyezwa isondele
Futhi uma ungababona lapho sebesaba, ngakho-ke angeke baphunyuke futhi bayobanjwa endaweni eseduzane
Futhi bayothi, “siyakholelwa kuyona” kepha bangakuthola kanjani lokho (iqiniso) besendaweni ekude na
Futhi ngempela abakholelwanga kulona (iqiniso) ngaphambilini futhi babengathekisa ngokungabonwayo basendaweni ekude
Futhi kuyobekwa okuhlukanisayo phakathi kwabo naloko abakufisayo njengoba kwenziwa kwabafananabo ngaphambilini, ngempela bona basekungabazeni okukhulu
Udumo lungolukaMvelinqangi umsunguli wamazulu nomhlaba owenza izingelosi izithunywa ezinamaphiko angambili nangantathu nangane uyakwandisa endalweni lokho akuthandayo, ngempela uMvelinqangi unamandla okwenza zonke izinto
Noma ngabe yini uMvelinqangi ayinikeza abantu emseni ngakho-ke akekho ongayigodla, futhi noma ngabe yini ayigodlayo akekho ongayikhulula ngemva kwakhe futhi yena uphakeme ngamandla unobuhlakani
Oh Bantu! khumbulani ububele bukaMvelinqangi kunina, ngakube ukhona yini omunye umdali ngaphandle kukaMvelinqangioninikaisabeloesivelaezulwininasemhlabeni na? Akekho onelungelo lokukhonzwa ngaphandle kwakhe, nimfulathelelani na
Futhi uma bekuphika ngempela zaziphikwa izithunywa ngaphambilini kwakho futhi ikuMvelinqangi lapho zibuyiselwa khona izindaba
Oh Bantu! ngempela isethembiso sikaMvelinqangi siyiqiniso ngakho-ke ayinganikhohlisi impilo yalomhlaba futhi akanganikhohlisi umkhohlisi ngoMvelinqangi
Ngempela usathane uyisitha senu, ngakho-ke mthatheni njengesitha kuphela umema iqembu lakhe ukuze libengabanye babangane bomlilo
Labo abangakholwanga okwabo yisijeziso esinzima. Futhi okwalaboabakholwayofuthiabenzaizenzoezinhleezilungileyo yintethelelo kanye nomvuzo omkhulu
Ngakube lowo owenzelwe izenzo zakhe ezimbi zabukeka zizinhle uzibona zizinhle ngakho-ke ngempela uMvelinqangi udukisa lowo amthandayo, futhi uholela (endleleni eqondile) lowo amthandayo, ngakho-ke awungaphatheki kabi umphefumulo wakho ngabo, ngempela uMvelinqangi uyisazi ngalokho abakwenzayo
Futhi nguMvelinqangi othumela imimoya bese iphakamisa amafu bese siwathumela ezweni elifile sivuse ngawo umhlaba emva kokufa kwawo, kunjalo ukuvuswa kokufileyo
Noma ngabe ngubani ofisa ukuhlonipheka ngakho-ke ukuhlonipheka konke kungokukaMvelinqangi, kuyena kukhuphukelaizwielihlekanyenomsebenziomuhleolungileyo uyalenyusa futhi labo abenza amacebo ngezinto ezimbi okwabo yisijeziso esinzima futhi icebo labo liyashabalala
Futhi uMvelinqangi wanidala ngothuli kwasekuba ingeconsi lesidoda wayesenenza nabangambili, futhi akekho owesifazane okhulelwe otetayo ngaphandle kolwazi lwakhe futhi akusikona ukuthi umuntu omdala welulelwa iminyaka noma incishiswe iminyaka yakhe kepha kusencwadini ngempela lokho kulula kuMvelinqangi
Futhi ulwandle olubili alufani lolu luhlwabusile lusashukela luyaphuzeka, loluya lusasawoti luyababa, kulona (lolubili) nidla inyama emnandi (izinhlanzi) futhi nikhipha imihlobiso eniyigqokayo futhi ubona imikhumbi ihamba kulona (ulwandle) ukuze nifune umusa wakhe futhi ukuze mhlawumbe nibonge
Wenza ukuthi ubusuku bungenele emini futhi wenza ukuthi imini ingenele ebusukwini futhi wenza ukuthi ilanga nenyanga ngakunye kuhambe isikhathi esinqunyiwe, lowo nguMvelinqangi iNkosi yenu, ubukhosi bungobakhe futhi labo enibamemezayo esikhundleni sakhe abanawo ngisho umucwana wohlamvu lwesundu
Uma nibamemeza abawuzwa umthandazo wenu futhi noma ngabe bayezwa abakwazi ukuniphendula futhi ngosuku lokuvuka kwabafileyo bayophika ukuzibandakanya kanye nani futhi akekho ongakutshela (lokhu) onjengonolwazi
Oh Bantu! Nina ningabadinga uMvelinqangi kepha yena uMvelinqangi akadingi lutho ungodunyiswayo
Uma ethanda anganisusa bese enza indalo entsha
Futhi lokho kuMvelinqangi akunzima
Futhi akekho umthwali wemithwalo oyothwala umthwalo womunye futhi uma omunye ethwele okusindayo ubiza omunye ukuthwala umthwalo wakhe, akekho oyothwala ingxenye kuwona ngisho noma ngabe yisihlobo esisondele, kuphela ungabaxwayisa labo abesaba iNkosi yabo engabonwayo futhi abenza umthandazo futhi noma ngabe ngubani ozihlanzayo kuphela uzihlanzela umphefumulo wakhe futhi sikuMvelinqangi isiphetho
Futhi akefani ongaboni nobonayo
Ngisho nobumnyama nokukhanya (akufani)
Ngisho nomthunzi nokushisa kwelanga (akufani)
Futhi abefani abaphilayo nabafileyo, ngempela uMvelinqangi wenza ukuthi ezwe lowo amthandayo futhi wena awusiyena owenza ukuthi bezwe labo abasemangcwabeni
Wena awuyilutho ngaphandle kokuba ngumxwayisi
Ngempela sakuthumela neqiniso njengomlethi wezindaba ezimnandi nomxwayisi, futhi asikho isizwe ekungazange kudlule kusona umxwayisi
Futhi uma bekuphika ngempela labo ababengaphambilini kwabo baphikwa, zafika kubona izithunywa zabo nezimpawu ezicacile nemibhalo kanye nencwadi ekhanyisayo
Ngabe sengiyababamba labo ababengakholwa (bheka) ukuthi kwakunjani ukubaphika kwami
Awuboni yini ukuthi uMvelinqangi wehlisela phansi amanzi avela esibhakabhakeni esiveza ngawo izithelo ezinemibala eyizinhlobonhlobo futhi ezintabeni kunezindlela ezimhlophe nezibomvu ezemibala eyehlukehlukene (ezinye) zimnyama kakhulu
Futhi phakathi kwabantu nasezilwaneni kanye nasezinkomeni kunemibala eyehlukehlukene, kuphela abesaba uMvelinqangi ezincekwini zakhe abanolwazi, ngempela uMvelinqangi uphakeme ngamandla ungothethelelayo
Ngempela labo abayifundayo incwadi kaMvelinqangi benze umthandazo futhi basebenzise (banikele) kulokho esababela kukona esithe nasobala bethembele ohwebweni olungasoze lwashabalala
Ukuze abakhokhele imivuzo yabo ngokugcwele futhi abanezelele emseni wakhe, ngempela yena uyathethelela uyabonga
Futhi loko esikwambulile kuwena kwencwadi kuyiqiniso eligcwalisela lokho okungaphambilini kwayo, ngempela uMvelinqangi uyazi uyazibona izinceku zakhe
Sabe sesibanikeza incwadi njengendlalifa labo esabakhethayo ezincekwini zethu, ngakho-ke phakathi kwabo kunalowo owona umphefumulo wakhe futhi phakathi kwabo kunalowo omaphakathi nendawo futhi phakathi kwabo kunalowo ophambili kunabo bonke ezenzweni ezinhle ngemvume kaMvelinqangi lokho kungumusa omkhulu
Izivande zangunaphakade abayongena kuzona, lapho phakathi bayohlotshiswa ngezigqizo zegolide nangobuhlalo futhi izingubo zabo lapho phakathi kuyoba ngezikasilika
Futhi bayothi, “udumo malube kuMvelinqangi okunguyena owasusa usizi kuthina! ngempela iNkosi yethu iyathethelela iyabonga”
(Inkosi) esihlalise endaweni yokuhlala yangunaphakade, ngomusa wayo futhi lapho phakathi angeke kusithinte ukusebenza futhi lapho phakathi angeke kusithinte ukukhathala
Futhi labo abangakholwanga okwabo ngumlilo wesihogo, asikho isikhathi esinqunyiwe kubona ukuthi bafe futhi angeke bancishiselwe esijezisweni sawo, sibanika umvuzo kanjalo bonke abangabongi
Futhi lapho phakathi bayokhalela (usizo) “Nkosi yethu sikhiphe sizokwenza izenzo ezinhle ezilungileyo hhayi lezo esasizenza” asizange yini sininike impilo ende ngokwanele ukuze noma ngabe ngubani owayengayaleka ayaleke na? Futhi wafika kunina umxwayisi, ngakho-ke yizwani abayizoni angeke babenaye umsizi
Ngempela uMvelinqangi uyisazi sokungabonwayo samazulu nomhlaba ngempela yena uyakwazi lokho okusezifubeni
Nguyena owanenza ukuba ngabalandelayo ngokuhlala emhlabeni. Ngakho-ke noma ngabe ngubani ongakholwa kukuyena ukungakholwa kwakhe futhi akubanezezeli abangakholwa ukungakholwa kwabo eNkosini yabo ngaphandle kokunengeka futhi akubanezeleli (ngalutho) abangakholwa ukungakholwa kwabo ngaphandle kokulahlekelwa
Ithi, “ngakube nibabonile yini abahlanganyeli benu labo enibabizayo esikhundleni sikaMvelinqangi na?, Ngikhombiseni ukuthi yini abayidalayo emhlabeni noma ngakube banomhlanganyeli emazulwini na? Noma ngakube sabanikeza incwadi bona basebufakazini obucacile kuyona na? Qhabo! izoni azithembisani lutho ngaphandle kwenkohliso”
Ngempela uMvelinqangi uyawabamba amazulu nomhlaba ukuthi angasuki endaweni yawo futhi uma esuka endaweni yawo akekho ngisho noyedwa ongawabamba womabili emva kwakhe ngempela yena ngasosonke isikhathi uyabekezela uyathethelela
Futhi bafunga ngoMvelinqangi izifungo zabo ezinqala ukuthi uma kungase kufike umxwayisi kubona bangaba ngabaholwe kakhulu ngaphezu kwanoma yiziphi izizwe kepha kwathi lapho sekufika umxwayisi kubona abazange banezelelwe yilutho ngaphandle kokukugwema lokho
Beqhosha emhlabeni futhi benza icebo elibi futhi icebo elibi alimsingathi omunye umuntu ngaphandle kwabantu balo ngakho-ke ngakube kukhona yini abakulindele ngaphandle kwendlela yasemandulo na? Kepha awusoze uyifumane inguquko endleleni kaMvelinqangi futhi awusoze ukufumane ukuchezuka endleleni kaMvelinqangi
Abazange yini bahambe ezweni babone ukuthi sasinjani isiphetho salabo ababengaphambilini kwabo futhi babeqatha ngamandla kunabo futhi uMvelinqangi akukho lutho elimphunyukayo emazulwini nasemhlabeni futhi yena ngasosonke isikhathi uyazi unamandla okwenza
Futhi ukube uMvelinqangi wayengase abajezise abantu ngenxa yalokho abakusebenzele wayengeke azishiye izidalwa ezinyakazayo (izilwane) phezu kwawo (umhlaba) kepha ubayekela isikhathi esinqunyiwe ngakho-ke uma kufika isikhathi sabo ngempela uMvelinqangi ngasosonke isikhathi ungumboni wezinceku zakhe

Futhi benzele isibonelo sabantu bedolobha ngenkathi kufika kulona izithunywa
Ngenkathi sithumela kubona (izithunywa) ezimbili base beyaziphika zombili sabe sesiyabaqinisa ngowesithathu basebethi “ngempela thina sithunyiwe kunina
Bathi (abantu bedolobha) “nina aniyilutho ngaphandle kokuba ngabantu abafana nathi futhi onomusa akazange ambule lutho kuphela nina niqamba amanga”
Zathi (izithunywa) “Inkosi yethu iyazi ukuthi thina siyizithunywa kunina”
Futhi alikho icala kuthina ngaphandle kokudlulisela umyalezo ocacile
Bathi, “ngempela thina sibona ukubikezela okubi kunina uma ningaphezi ngempela sizonikhanda ngamatshe futhi nizothintwa yisijeziso esibuhlungu esivela kuthina”
Zathi (izithunywa), “ukubikezela kwenu kukanye nani ngoba nikhunjuzisiwe kepha nina ningabantu abephula umthetho”
Futhi kwafika indoda ivela engxenyeni ebuqamama yedolobha igijima yathi “Oh Bantu bami! landelani izithunywa”
Landelani labo abangawuceli umvuzo kunina futhi bona bangabaholelwe endleleni elungileyo
Futhi kungani ukuthi ngingamkhonzi lowo owangidalayo futhi niyobubuyiselwa kuyena
Ngakube ngingazithathela omunye uNkulunkulu wamanga esikhundleni sakhe kulapho onomusa ehlose inhlupheko kumina na?, angeke kungisize ngalutho ukungincengela kwabo futhi angeke bangisindise
Ngempela mina ngiyobe ngisekudukeni okucacile
Ngempela mina ngikholiwe eNkosini yenu ngakho-ke ngilaleleni
Kwathiwa, “ngena esivandeni (ezulwini)” wathi, “ngifisa sengathi abantu bami bangazi”
Ngokuthi iNkosi yami ingithethelele futhi yangibeka kanye nabahloniphekileyo
Futhi asiyehliselanga phezulu kwabantu bakhe emva kwakhe impi evela ezulwini futhi kwakungadingeki ukuthi siyithumele
Kwakungeyilutho kepha kwakungumsindo owodwa masinyane babethule du
Oh ukuzisola ebantwini! Kwakungakaze kufike kubona isithunywa ngaphandle kokuthi babesenza inhlekisa
Ngakube ababoni yini ukuthi zingaki izizukulwane esazibhubhisa ngaphambilini kwabo zona angeke zibuyele kubona
Futhi ngempela bonke-bonke bayolethwa ngaphambili kwethu
Futhi uphawu lwabo umhlaba ofile sawuphilisa sabe sesiveza kuwona uhlamvu kuze badle kulona
Futhi kuwona sazenza izivande zamasundu nezamagilebhisi futhi kuwona sayenza imithombo ukuthi iqhume
Ukuze badle ezithelweni zawo futhi izandla zabo azizitshalanga (izithelo) ngakube ababongi yini na
Udumo malube kulowo owadala kwaba ngakubili kukona konke okuvezwa umhlaba kanye nokohlobo lwabo nakulokho abangakwazi
Futhi uphawu lwabo ubusuku, siyalukhipha usuku kubona kulapho bona besebumnyameni
Futhi ilanga lihamba njalo liya lapho liphelela khona, lokho kungempoqo yophakeme ngamandla oyisazi
Nenyanga siyinqumele izimo ezibonakalayo kuze kube yilapho iphenduka iba njengegatsha lesundu elidala elomile
Akusikhona okwelanga ukuthi lifice inyanga noma ubusuku ukuthi budlule imini futhi konke kuhamba emkhondweni
Futhi uphawu lwabo ukuthi sayithwala inzalo yabo emkhunjini othweleyo
Futhi sibadalele okufana nako, lokhu abakugibelayo
Futhi uma sithanda singabaminzisa ngakho-ke angeke balekelelwe futhi bona angeke bahlengwe
Ngaphandle komusa ovela kuthina kanye nenjabulo yesikhashana
Futhi uma kuthiwa kubona “qaphelani loko okungaphambili kwenu kanye nalokho okungemumva kwenu ukuze mhlawumbe nithole umusa”
Futhi alifiki kubona ivesi emavesini eNkosi yabo ngaphandle kokuba bayalifulathela
Futhi uma kuthiwa kubona “sebenzisani kulokho anabela kona uMveliqangi” labo abangakholwanga bathi kulabo abakholwayo “ngakube singodla lowo okungathi uma ethanda uMvelinqangi amondle?” Anikwiyilutho ngaphandle kokuba sephutheni eligqamile
Futhi bathi, “siyofika nini lesisithembiso uma kungukuthi nina niqinisile?”
Abalindele lutho ngaphandle kokukhala okukodwa okuyobathatha kulapho bona bephikisana
Ngakho-ke angeke bakwazi ukwenza ifa noma ukubuyela ebantwini babo
Futhi liyoshawa icilongo kulapho bona beyophuma emathuneni beshesha bebheke eNkosini yabo
Bayothi, “Oh usizi kuthina! Ngubani lowo osivuse endaweni yethu, lokhu kuyilokhu onomusa akwethembisa nezithunywa zakhuluma iqiniso”
Angeke kube yilutho ngaphandle kokukhala okukodwa kulapho bona bonke beyolethwa ngaphambili kwethu
Ngakho-ke ngalolusuku umphefumulo angeke wenziwe okungenabo ubulungiswa ngalutho futhi angeke ninikwe umvuzo ngaphandle kwaloko enanikwenza
Ngempela izihlali zesivande kulolosuku ziyobamatasatasa ngezinto eziyinjabulo
Bona kanye namakhosikazi abo bayoba semthunzini, bacambalale endaweni ephakeme
Okwabo lapho phakathi yizithelo futhi okwabo kuyoba yinoma ngabe yini abayicelayo
Ukuthula! Izwi elivela eNkosini enesihawu
Futhi hlukanani namuhla Oh nina eniyizoni
Angizange yini nginiphoqe Oh bantwana ba-Adam! Ukuthi ningamkhonzi usathane? Ngempela yena uyisitha senu esigqamile
Nokuthi nikhonze mina? Lena yindlela elungile
Futhi ngempela wadukisa iqembu elikhulu phakathi kwenu ngakube naningenawo yini umqondo
Lesi yisihogo enanethenjiswe sona
Ngenani kusona namhlanje ngenxa yokuthi naningakholwa
Kulolusuku siyayisicilela imilomo yabo futhi izandla zabo zizokhuluma nezinyawo zabo zizofakaza mayelana naloko ababekusebenzela
Futhi ukube besithanda besizosusa amehlo abo bese beyaphuphutheka endleleni bese bebona kanjani
Futhi ukube besithanda besizobaguqula ezindaweni zabo bebengeke besakwazi ukuya phambili nokuphindela emumva
Futhi noma ngabe ngubani esimnika impilo ende simhlehlisela emumva endalweni, ngakube abanawo yini umqondo na
Futhi asimfundisanga ubumbongi futhi akumfanele, yona ayiyilutho ngaphandle kwesikhumbuzo neQur’an ecacile
Ukuze ixwayise noma ngabe ngubani ophilayo futhi kuqiniseke izwi ukubhekana nabangakholwa
Ababoni yini ukuthi sabadalela kuloko okwenziwe yizandla zethu izinkomo abangabanini bazo na
Futhi sabathobisela zona ngakho-ke ezinye phakathi kwazo bayazigibela futhi ezinye phakathi kwazo bayazidla
Futhi banenzuzo kuzona kanye neziphuzo, ngakube ababongi yini na
Futhi esikhundleni sikaMvelinqangi bazithathela izithixo ukuze mhlawumbe bathole usizo
Azikwazi ukubasiza futhi bona kuzona bayibutho elilethwe ngaphambili
Ngakho-ke ayingakuphathi kabi inkulumo yabo ngempela thina siyakwazi lokho abakufihlayo kanye nalokho abakuveza obala
Ngakube umuntu akaboni yini ukuthi samdala ngeconsi lesidoda kulapho yena eyisitha esigqamile
Futhi wasenzela isibonelo wakhohlwa yindalo yakhe wathi, “ngubani onika amathambo impilo uma esewuthuli na?”
Ithi, “uwanika impilo lowo owadalayo ngesikhathi sokuqala futhi yena uyisazi sazona zonke izidalwa”
Lowo owanibekela umlilo esihlahleni esiluhlaza kulapho nina nokhela kuwona
Angeke yini lowo owadala amazulu nomhlaba akwazi ukudala okufana nabo na? Yebo! Yena ungumdali owaziyo
Kuphela, impoqo yakhe, uma ehlose into ethize uthi kuyona “yenzeka” bese iyenzeka

Ngempela uMvelinqangi wenu munye
INkosi yamazulu nomhlaba kanye nako konke okuphakathi kwako kokubili neNkosi yempumalanga
Ngempela thina salihlobisa izulu eliseduzane ngomhlobiso wezinkanyezi
Nokulondolozwa	kwalo	mayelana	nabobonke	osathane abahlubukayo

Bayaxoshwa futhi okwabo yisijeziso sangunaphakade
Ngaphandle kwalowo ohlwitha okuthize ngokuntshontsha bese elandelwa yilangabi lomlilo elihlabayo

Kepha uyamangala kulapho benza inhlekisa

Wathi (uDavide), “ngempela wenze okungenabo ubulungiswa kuwena ngokufuna imvukazi yakho ezimvukazini zakhe futhi ngempela baningi abahlanganyeli abacindezelana bodwa ngaphandle kwalabo abakholwayo futhi abenza okulungileyo futhi bambalwa labo” futhi uDavide wabona ukuthi simlingile, ngakho-ke wacela intethelelo eNkosini yakhe, wawa phansi wazithoba futhi waphendukela kuMvelinqangi ngokuzisola

Wathi, “ngakho-ke ngokuhlonipheka kwakho ngempela ngizobadukisa bonke”
Ngaphandle kwezinceku zakho ezikhethiwe phakathi kwabo
Wathi, “yiqiniso futhi yiqiniso engilishoyo”
Ngempela ngizogcwalisa isihogo ngawe kanye nangabobonke abakulandelayo phakathi kwabo
Ithi anginiceli umvuzo ngako futhi mina angiyena omunye wabakhohlisi
Akuyilutho ngaphandle kwesikhumbuzo emihlabeni. 89. Futhi ngempela nizozazi izindaba zaso emva kwesikhashana
Isambulo sencwadi sivela kuMvelinqangi ophakeme ngamandla onobuhlakani
Ngempela sayembula kuwena incwadi ngeqiniso, ngakho-ke khonza uMvelinqangi ube qotho kuyena enkolweni
Ngokungangabazeki, ingekaMvelinqangi inkolo eqotho futhi labo abazithathele abavikeli esikhundleni sakhe (bathi) kuphela sibakhonzela ukuthi basisondeze eduzane noMvelinqangi ngempela uMvelinqangi akamholi lowo ongumqambi manga ongabongi
Ukube uMvelinqangi wayethanda ukuthatha indondana wayezokhetha kulokho akudalayo akuthandayo, udumo malube kuye! Yena unguMvelinqangi oyedwa umnqobi
Wadala amazulu nomhlaba ngeqiniso, wenza ukuthi ubusuku bumboze imini futhi wenza ukuthi imini imboze ubusuku futhi wenza ilanga nenyanga kwathoba, konke kuhamba ngesikhathi esinqunyiwe ngokungangabazeki yena ungophakeme ngamandla ungothethelelayo
Wanidala ngomphefumulo owodwa wabe esenza ngaye unkosikazi wakhe futhi wanehlisela phansi imfuyo engambili eyisishiyagalombili, unidala eziswini zabomama benu, indalo emva kwendalo ebumnyameni obuphindiwe kathathu lowo nguMvelinqangi iNkosi yenu bungobakhe ubukhosi akekho uNkulunkulu onokukhonzwa ngaphandle kwakhe ngakho-ke niphendukiselwa kanjani emumva
Uma ningakholwa ngakho-ke ngempela uMvelinqangi akanidingi futhi akakuthandi ukungakholwa ezincekwini zakhe futhi uma nibonga uyakuthokozela kunina, futhi akekho umthwali womthwalo oyothwala umthwalo womunye bese kuba seNkosini yenu ukubuyela kwenu bese iyanitshela ngaloko enanikwenza, ngempela yona iyisazi saloko okusezifubeni
Futhi uma umuntu ethintwa ukhala kumvelinqangi ebheka kuye ecela intethelelo, kepha uma emupha emuseni wakhe, (umuntu) uyakhohlwa ukuthi ubekhala ngokuthintwa kwakhe, bese enza abahlanganyeli kanye no Mvelinqangi edukisa abantu kude nendlela ka-Allah. Ithi, “kujabulele nkungakholwa kwakho, nina yinina eningabangane besi hogo.”
Kungabelowooqothophakathikobusukueguqilengokuzithoba futhi emile uqaphela impilo ezayo futhi uthembele emseni weNkosi yakhe ithi, “ngakube bayalingana yini labo abaziyo kanye nalabo abangazi na?” Kuphela yilabo abakhumbulayo abantu abaqondayo abathola ukukukweluleka
Ithi, “Oh zinceku zami! lezo ezikholwayo yesabani iNkosi yenu” okwalabo abenza okuhle kakhulu kulomhlaba futhi umhlaba kaMvelinqangi ubanzi kuphela yilabo ababekezelayo abayokwemukela umvuzo wabo ngaphandle kwesibalo
Ithi, “ngempela mina ngiphoqiwe ukuthi ngikhonze uMvelinqangi ngibeqotho enkolweni yakhe”
Futhi ngiphoqiwe ukuba ngibe ngowokuqala wabazinikele ngaphansi kwentando kaMvelinqangi
Ithi, “ngempela mina ngiyesaba isijeziso sosuku olukhulu uma ngingayihloniphi iNkosi yami”
Ithi, “uMvelinqangi engimkhonzayo ngiqotho enkolweni yakhe”
Ngakho-ke khonzani loko enikuthandayo esikhundleni sakhe, ithi ngempela abalahlekelwe yilabo abalahlekelwe yimiphefumulo yabo kanye nabantu babo ngosuku lokuvuka kwabafileyo, ngempela loko ukulahlekelwa okucacile
Okwabo kuyoba uphahla lomlilo ngaphezulu kwabo futhi nangaphansi kwabo izembozo (zomlilo) loko uMvelinqangi wesabisa ngako izinceku zakhe, Oh zinceku zami! ngakho-ke ngesabeni
Futhi labo abagwema izithixo hleze bazikhonze bese bephendukela kuMvelinqangi okwabo yizindaba ezinhle ngakho-ke memezela izindaba ezinhle ezincekwini zami
Labo abalalela inkulumo bese belandela okuhle kwayo labo- ke bayilabo abaholwa nguMvelinqangi futhi labo bangabantu abaqondayo
Ngakube lowo eliqinisekile kuyena igama lesijeziso, ngakube wena ungamsindisa yini lowo osemlilweni
Kepha labo abayesabayo iNkosi yabo okwabo ngamagumbi adephile elinye ngaphezulu kwelinye ngaphansi kwawo kugelezaimifula, yisethembisosikaMvelinqangi, uMvelinqangi akehluleki esethembisweni
Awuboni yini ukuthi uMvelinqangi wehlisela phansi amanzi avela esibhakabhakeni bese ewenza ukuthi angene ageleze njengeziphethu emhlabeni bese eveza ngawo izithelo ezinemibala eyehlukahlukene bese ziyabuna uzibone zibaphuzi bese ezenza ziba yizicucu, ngempela kuloko kunesikhumbuzo kubantu abaqondayo
Ngakube lowo uMvelinqangi avule isifuba sakhe esivulela i-Islam (ukuzinikela ngaphansi kwentando kaMvelinqangi) usekukhanyeni okuvela eNkosini yakhe? ngakho-ke usizi kulabo izinhliziyo zabo ezilukhuni esikhumbuzweni, labo basekudukeni okucacile
NguMvelinqangi owehlisela phansi inkulumo enhle kakhulu incwadi ziyefana ziphindaphindiwe, izikhumba zalabo abesaba iNkosi yabo ziyathuthumela bngayo bese izikhumba zabo kanye nezinhliziyo zabo ziyathamba enkumbulweni kaMvelinqangi, lokho ngukuhola kukaMvelinqangi, uhola ngako lowo amthandayo, futhi lowo uMvelinqangi amdukisayo ngakho-ke angeke abenaye umholi
Ngakube lowo oyobhekana ngobuso bakhe nesijeziso esibi ngosuku lokuvuka kwabafileyo futhi kuyothiwa kwabayizoni yizwani loko nina enanikusebanzela
Baphika labo ababengaphambilini kwabo ngakho-ke safika kubona isijeziso siqhamuka lapho bengaboni khona
Ngakho-ke uMvelinqangi wabazwisa ihlazo empilweni yakulomhlaba futhi ngempela isijeziso sempilo ezayo sikhulu kakhulu ukube bebazi
Futhi ngempela sabenzela abantu izibonelo kuleQur’an zazozonke izinhlobo ukuze bakhumbule
IQur’an engesi-Arabhu engenabo ubuzombezombe ukuze bamesabe (uMvelinqangi)
UMvelinqangi wenza isibonelo sendoda ephethwe ngabahlanganyeli abaphikisanayo kanye nendoda ephethwe ngokuphelele ngumphathi (oyedwa) ngakube bobabili bayefana? Udumiso malube kuMvelinqangi kepha iningi labo alazi
Ngempela uzokufa futhi ngempela nabo bazokufa
Bese ngempela nina ngosuku lokuvuka kwabafileyo niyaphikisana ngaphambili kweNkosi yenu
Ngakho-ke ngubani ongalungile kakhulu kunalowo oqambela uMvelinqangi amanga futhi aphike iqiniso kulapho selimfikele na? kanti akuson yini isihogo indawo yokuhlala abangakholwa na
Futhi lowo olethe iqiniso futhi akholelwe kulona labo bangabamesabayo Umvelinqangi
Okwabo kuyoba yinoma ngabe yintoni abayifisayo eNkosini yabo lowo ngumvuzo wabenzi bokuhle
Ukuze uMvelinqangi asuse kubona okubi kakhulu kwaloko ababekwenza futhi abanike umvuzo wabo ngokuhle kakhulu kwaloko ababekwenza
Ngakube uMvelinqangi akayanele yini inceku yakhe na? futhi bakwesabisa ngalabo (abakhonza abanye) esikhundleni sakhe futhi noma ngabe ngubani uMvelinqangi amshiya ekudukeni ngakho-ke akanaye umholi
Futhi lowo oholwa nguMvelinqangi ngakho-ke akanaye umdukisi, akusiyena yini na uMvelinqangi ophakeme ngamandla ongumnini wokuphindisela
Futhi uma ubabuza ukuthi ngubani owadala amazulu nomhlaba ngempelabazothi“ nguMvelinqangi” ithi“ ngakubenikubonile yini loko enikubizayo esikhundleni sikaMvelinqangi uma uMvelinqangi efisa ukungihlupha ngakube loko kungakususa ukuhlupha kwakhe na? noma uma efisa ukungikhombisa umusa ngakube loko kungawugodla yini umusa wakhe na?” ithi “ uMvelinqangi unganele, bathembela kuyena abethembeli”
Ithi “Oh Bantu bami! Sebenzani ngendlela yenu, ngempela nami ngiyisisebenzi ngakho-ke niyokwazi
Ukuthi ngubani esiza kuyena isijeziso esidumazayo futhi esivumeleke kuyena isijeziso esingapheliyo
Ngempela sayembula kuwena incwadi siyembulela abantu ngeqiniso ngakho-ke noma ngabe ngubani oholekile kungokomphefumulo wakhe futhi noma ngabe ngubani odukayo kuphela uzidukela yena futhi wena awusiyena umgadi wabo
UMvelinqangi uyayithatha imiphefumulo ngesikhathi sokufa kwayo kanye naleyo engafi ekulaleni kwayo bese eyayigodla leyo ayinqumele ukufa bese ethumela eminye esikhathini esinqunyiwe, ngempela kulokhu kunezimpawu kubantu abaziyo
Noma ngakube bazithathela abancengeli esikhundleni sikaMvelinqangi? Ithi “ngisho noma ngabe bengenalutho futhi bengenawo umqondo
Ithi,“kungokukaMvelinqangikonkeukuncengela, ungowakhe umbuso wamazulu nomhlaba bese nibuyiselwa kuyena”
Futhi uma uMvelinqangi ekhunjulwa yedwa ziyashwabana izinhliziyo zalabo abangakholelwa empilweni ezayo kepha uma kukhunjulwa labo abanye esikhundleni sakhe yilapho bona bejabula
Ithi “Oh Mvelinqangi msunguli wamazulu nomhlaba isazi sokungabonwa nokubonwayo wena wehlulela phakathi kwezinceku zakho kuloko eziphikisana kukona”
Futhi noma ngabe okwalabo abangalungile yikona konke okusemhlabeni kanye nokufana nako kanye nako banganikela ngako njengenhlengo ebubini besijeziso sosuku lokuvuka kwabafileyo futhi kuyoba sobala kubona kuvela kuMvelinqangi loko abangakucabanganga
Futhi kuyovela obala kubona ububi lobo ababusebenzela futhi kuyoqiniseka kubona loko ababenza ngako inhlekisa
Kepha uma umuntu ethintwa ukulimala umemeza thina kuthi lapho uma simnika ububele obuvela kuthina athi kuphela nginikwe bona ngenxa yolwazi lwami qhabobo yisivivinyo kepha iningi labo alazi
Ngempela bakusho loko labo ababengaphambilini kwabo ngakho-ke akuzange kubasize loko ababekusebenzela
Ngakho-ke behlelwa okubi ababekusebenzela futhi labo abangalungile phakathi kwalabo bayokwehlelwa okubi abakusebenzela futhi bona angeke baphunyuke
Abazi yini ukuthi uMvelinqangi uyaselula isabelo kulowo amthandayo Futhiasinciphise, ngempelakulokokunezimpawu kubantu abakholwayo
Ithi “Oh zinceku zami! Lezo ezazimosha imiphefumulo yazo, ningapheli ithemba emseni kaMvelinqangi, ngempela uMvelinqangi uyazithethelela zonke izono, ngempela yena ungothethelelayo onesihawu”
Futhi phendukelani eNkosini yenu nizinikele kuyona ngaphambi kokuba isijeziso sifike kunina bese ningabi nakusizwa
Futhi landelani okuhle kakhulu loko okwembulwa kunina okuvela eNkosini yenu ngaphambi kokuba sifike kunina isijeziso ngokuphazima kulapho nina ningaboni
Hleze umphefumulo uthi, “Oh ukuzisola kwami kuloko engangingakunakile mayelana noMvelinqangi futhi ngangingomunye walabo ababenza inhlekisa”
Noma uthi, “ukube uMvelinqangi wayengiholile ngangizoba ngomunye wabalungileyo”
Noma uthi ngenkathi ubona isijeziso, “ukube bengingaba nelinye ithuba bengingaba ngomunye wabenzi bokuhle”
Yebo! Ngempela amavesi ami afika kuwena kepha wawaphika futhi waqhosha wabe sewuba ngomunye wabangakholwa
Futhi ngosuku lokuvuka kwabafileyo uyobona labo ababeqambela uMvelinqangi amanga ubuso babo buyobe benziwe mnyama, esihogweni ayikho yini indawo yokuhlala abaziphakamisayo
Futhi uMvelinqangi uyobasindisa labo abenza okulungileyo ngenxa yempumelelo yabo angeke bathintwe wokubi futhi bona angeke baphatheke kabi
UMvelinqangi ngumdali wezinto zonke futhi yena ungumgadi ngaphezulu kwezinto zonke
Ngezakhe izihluthulelo zamazulu nomhlaba futhi labo abangakholelwa emavesini kaMvelinqangi labo-ke bangabalahlekelwe
Ithi, “ngakube ningiphoqelela ekukhonzeni abanye onkulunkulu okungesiyena uMvelinqangi Oh nina eningazi”
Futhi ngempela kwembulwa kuwena kanye nakulabo ababengaphambilini kwakho, uma wenzele uMvelinqangi abahlanganyeli ekumkhonzeni izenzo zakho zizobayize bese ubakulabo abalahlekelwe
Ngakho-ke khonza uMvelinqangi futhi ube ngomunye wababongayo
Futhi abasenzi isilinganiso (ngobunjalo) bukaMvelinqangi ngendlela ayiyona Futhi umhlaba wonke uyowubamba ngosuku lokuvuka kwabafileyo futhi amazulu ayogoqwa esandleni sakhe sokudla, udumo malube kuye futhi uphakeme ngaphezulu kwaloko ababekwenza abahlanganyeli ekumkhonzeni
Futhikuyokhaliswaicilongobesebeyafabonkeabasemazulwini nabobonke abasemhlabeni ngaphandle kwalabo ngokuthanda kukaMvelinqangi bese liyakhaliswa ngesinye isikhathi bese kuba yilapho besukuma belinda
Futhi umhlaba uyocwebezela ngokukhanya kweNkosi futhi incwadi iyobekwa phansi futhi kuyolethwa abaphrofethi kanye nabofakazi, futhi kuyokwehlulelwa phakathi kwabo ngeqiniso futhi bona angeke benziwe okungenabo ubulungiswa
Futhi umphefumulo nomphefumulo uyokhokhelwa ngokuphelele loko owakwenza futhi yena (uMvelinqangi) wazi kangcono ngalokho ababekwenza
Futhi labo abangakholwanga bayolethwa esihogweni beyizixuku kuze kube yilapho befika kusona futhi iyovulwa iminyango yaso futhi bayothi kubona abaqaphi baso “ngakube azifikanga yini kunina izithunywa eziphuma phakathi kwenu zinifundela amavesi eNkosi yenu futhi zinixwayisa ngokuhlangana kwalolusuku lwenu na?” bayothi “yebo” kepha liyogcwaliseka izwi lesijeziso kwabangakholwa
Kuyothiwa, “ngenani eminyangweni yesihogo nihlale lapho phakathi ingunaphakade, yimbi indawo yokuhlala abaqholoshayo”
Futhi labo abayesabayo iNkosi yabo bayolethwa esivandeni (ezulwini) beyizixuku kuze kube yilapho befika kulona futhi iyovulwa iminyango yalo futhi bayothi kubona abaqaphi balo “ukuthula makube kunina nenza kahle ngakho-ke ngenani kulona ingunaphakade”
Futhi bayothi “udumo malube kuMvelinqangi osifezile kuthina isethembiso sakhe futhi usenze saba yizindlalifa zezwe, sihlale ezulwini noma ngabe yikuphi lapho sithanda khona, muhle kakhulu umvuzo wabasebenzi
Futhiuyobonaizingelosizizungelezeisihlalo(sikaMvelinqangi) sobukhosi zigubha indumiso yeNkosi yazo futhi kuyokwehlulelwa phakathi kwazo ngeqiniso Futhi kuyothiwa “Udumo malube kuMvelinqangi iNkosi yemihlaba”
Ha Meem
Isambulo sencwadi sivela kuMvelinqangi ophakeme ngamandla oyisazi
Umthetheleli wesono nomamukeli wokuzisola, onzima ekujeziseni, umnikazi womusa, ayikho into enokukhonzwa ngaphandle kwakhe kukuyena ukubuyela
Abekho abaphikisanayo ngamavesi kaMvelinqangi ngaphandle kwalabo abangakholwanga ngakho-ke akungakukhohlisi ukuzulazula kwabo ezweni
Abantu baNowa baphika ngaphambilini kwabo kanye namaqembu emva kwabo futhi zonke izizwe zahlosa ukuphambana nesithunywa sazo ukuze zisibambe Futhi ziphikise ngamanga ukuze zenze ngawo iqiniso libe yize ngakho-ke ngabathatha sasinjani isijeziso sami
Futhi kanjalo laqiniseka izwi leNkosi yakho kulabo abangakholwanga ukuthi bona bangabangane bomlilo
Labo abathwele isihlalo sobukhosi kanye nalabo abasizungelezile, bagubha indumiso yeNkosi yakho futhi bakholelwa kuyona futhi bacelela labo abakholwayo intethelelo Nkosi yethu wengamele zonke izinto ngomusa nangolwazi ngakho-ke bathethelele labo abazisolayo futhi abalandela indlela yakho futhi baphephise esijezisweni sesihogo
Nkosi yethu bangenise ezivandeni zaphakade lezo owabathembisa zona kanye noma ngabe ngubani olungile phakathi kobaba babo namakhosikazi abo kanye nenzalo yabo, ngempela wena ungophakeme ngamandla onobuhlakani
Futhi bavikele ebubini futhi noma ngabe ngubani omvikelayo ebubini ngalolusuku ngempela unomusa kuyena futhi lokho kuyimpumelelo enkulu
Ngempela labo abangakholwanga bayobizwa “ngempela inzondo kaMvelinqangi yinkulu kakhulu kunenzondo yenu kunina uqobo ngenkathi nibizelwa enkolweni kepha nanenqaba
Bathi Nkosi yethu usenze ukuthi sife kabili futhi wasiphilisa kabili ngakho-ke siyazivuma izono zethu, ngakube ikhona yini indlela yokuphuma na
Lokho kungenxa yokuthi ngenkathi uMvelinqangi emenyezwa yedwa anizange nikholwe kepha kwathi uma behlanganiswa naye abahlanganyeli nabe seniyakholwa ngakho-ke ukwehlulela kungokukaMvelinqangi ophakeme omkhulu
Nguyena onikhombisa izimpawu zakhe futhi onehlisela phansi isabelo esivela ezulwini futhi akekho okhumbulayo ngaphandle kwalowo ophendukayo
Ngakho-ke bizani uMvelinqangi nibe qotho kuyena enkolweni yize noma ngabe bengakuthandi loko abangakholwa
Uphakeme ngamazinga, umnikazi wesihlalo sobukhosi, wenza ukuthi umoya wehlele kulowo amthandayo ezincekwini zakhe ngempoqo yakhe ukuze axwayise ngosuku lokuhlangana
Ngosuku abayovela ngalo, akukho lutho olwabo oluyofihleka kuMvelinqangi, ungokabani umbuso ngalolusuku na? ungokaMvelinqangi oyedwa umnqobi
Ngalolusuku yonke imiphefumulo izonikwa umvuzo ngalokho ekusebenzele angeke kwenziwe okungenabo ubulungiswa ngalolusuku, ngempela uMvelinqangi uyashesha ekubaleni
Futhi baxwayise ngosuku olusondelayo lapho izinhliziyo ziyobe zisemiphinjeni, abangalungile angeke babe nomngane futhi angeke babenomncengeli oyohlonishwa
Uyakwazi okungumkhohlisi wamehlo kanye naloko okufihlwa yisifuba
Futhi uMvelinqangi wehlulela ngeqiniso futhi labo abababizayo esikhundleni sakhe abehluleli lutho! Ngempela uMvelinqangi ungozwayo obonayo
Abazange yini bahambe emhlabeni ukuze babone ukuthi sasinjani isiphetho salabo ababengaphambilini kwabo bona babenamandla amakhulu kunabo futhi beqatha uMvelinqangi ngezono zabo futhiabazange babenaye owayezobavikela kuMvelinqangi
Lokho kungenxa yokuthi zazifika kubona izithunywa zabo namavesi acacile kepha abakholwanga ngakho-ke uMvelinqangi wababamba ngempela yena unamandla, unzima ekujeziseni
Futhi ngempela samthumela uMose namavesi ethu kanye negunya elicacile
Kufaro nakuHaman nakuKarun ngakho-ke bathi “umlumbi onamanga”
Ngakho-ke kwathi lapho esebafikela neqiniso elivela kuthina bathi “bulalani amadodana alabo abakholwayo kanye naye, niyeke abesifazane babo” futhi icebo labangakholwa aliyilutho ngaphandle kokuduka
Futhi uFaro wathi “ngiyekeni ngimbulale uMose ukuze abize iNkosi yakhe ngempela mina ngiyesaba ukuthi uzoyiguqula inkolo yenu noma enze ukuganga emhlabeni”
Futhi uMose wathi “ngempela mina ngifune isiphephelo eNkosini yami neNkosi yenu kubona bonke abaziqhenyayo akakholelwa osukwini lokubala (lokwahlulela)”
Futhi indoda ekholwayo emndenini kaFaro eyayifihle ukholo lwayo yathi ngakube nibulala indoda ngenxa yokuthi ithi “iNkosi yami nguMvelinqangi futhi ngempela inilethele izimpawu ezicacile ezivela eNkosini yenu, futhi uma iqamba amanga ngakho-ke aphezulu kwayo amanga ayo futhi uma ineqiniso nizokwehlelwa okunye kwaloko anethembisa kona ngempela uMvelinqangi akamholi lowo omoshayo ongumqambimanga
Oh Bantu bami! Ungowenu umbuso namhlanje ningababusi emhlabeni ngakho-ke ngubani ozosivikela esijezisweni sikaMvelinqangi uma sifika kuthina? UFaro wathi, “anginikhombisi lutho ngaphandle kwengikubonayo futhi anginiholeli (kwenye indawo) ngaphandle kwasendleleni yokulunga”
Futhi lowo owayekholwa wathi “Oh bantu bami! ngempela mina ngiyanesabela okufana nosuku lwezixuku”
Njengesiphetho sabantu baNowa naba A’d nabaThamud kanye nalabo ababengemumva kwabo futhi uMvelinqangi akakuthandi ukungabi nobulungiswa ezincekwini
Futhi Oh Bantu bami! Ngempela mina ngiyanesabela usuku lokubizana
Ngosuku eniyofulathela ngalo nibaleka, aninaye umvikeli kuMvelinqangi futhi lowo odukiswa nguMvelinqangi ngakho- ke akanaye umholi
Futhi ngempela uJosefa wafika kunina ngaphambilini nezimpawu ezicacile kepha naqhubeka nokuba sekungabazeni kuloko ayenifikele nako, kwaze kwaba uyafa nathi “uMvelinqangi akasoze asithumele isithunywa ngemva kwakhe” Kanjalo uMvelinqangi umshiya ekudukeni lowo omoshayo ongabazayo
Labo abaphikisanayo ngamavesi kaMvelinqangi ngaphandle kwegunya elafika kubona, kuzonde kakhulu kuMvelinqangi kanye nakulabo abakholwayo kanjalo uMvelinqangi uyayisicilela inhliziyo yalowo nalowo oqhoshayo ocindezelayo
Futhi uFaro wathi, “Oh Haman! Ngakhele isakhiwo esiphakeme ukuze ngithole izindlela”
Izindlela zezulu ukuze ngikhuphukele kuNkulunkulu kaMose futhi ngempela ngicabanga ukuthi ungumqambi manga futhi kanjalo kwenziwa kuFaro babukeka bubuhle ububi bomsebenzi wakhe wayesevinjelwa endleleni futhi icebo likaFaro lalingeyilutho ngaphandle kokubhubha
Futhi lowo owayekholwa wathi, “Oh Bantu bami! ngilandeleni ngizoniholela endleleni elungile”
Oh Bantu bami! Kuphela lempilo yalomhlaba yinjabulo futhi ngempela impilo ezayo yindawo yokuphumula
Noma ngabe ngubani owenza okubi angeke anikwe umvuzo ngaphandle kokufana nako futhi noma ngabe ngubani owenza okulungileyo engowesilisa noma engowesifazane futhi yena eyikholwa ngakho-ke labo bayongena esivandeni (ezulwini) bayokwabelwa khona ngaphandle kwesilinganiso
Futhi Oh Bantu bami! Kungani ukuthi mina nginimemela ensindisweni kulapho nina ningimemela emlilweni
Ningimemela ukuthi ngingakholwa kuMvelinqangi futhi ngimenzele abahlanganyeli ekumkhonzeni lokho engingenalo ulwazi lwako futhi mina nginimemela kophakeme ngamandla umthetheleli
Ngempela ningibizela kuloko ekungafanelwe kubizwe kulomhlaba ngisho nasempilweni ezayo	futhi ukuphindela kwethu kukuMvelinqangi futhi izoni zona zingabangane bomlilo
Ngakho-ke niyokukhumbula loko engikushoyo kunina, futhi udaba lwami ngilubeka kuMvelinqangi, ngempela uMvelinqangi ungumboni wezinceku
Ngakho-ke uMvelinqangi wamvikela ebubini balokho ababekuceba futhi saqiniseka kubantu baFaro isijeziso esibi
Umlilo bayolethwa kuwona ekuseni nakusihlwa futhi ngosuku eliyofika ngalo ihora (kuyothiwa) “ngenisani abantu baFaro esijezisweni esinzima”
Futhi khumbula ngenkathi beyophikisana emlilweni ngakho- ke bayothi ababuthakathaka kulabo ababezigabisa “ngempela thina sasingabalandeli benu ngakube nizoyiqhelelanisa nathi yini na ingxenye yomlilo?”
Bayothi labo ababezigabisa, “ngempela sonke siphakathi kuwona, ngempela uMvelinqangi uyehlulela phakathi kwezinceku”
Futh labo abasemlilweni bayothi kubagadi besihogo, “bizani iNkosi yenu isenzele lula isijeziso sosuku olulodwa”
Bayothi, “azizange yini na zifike kunina izithunywa zenu namavesi acacile?” bayothi,“yebo” bayothi “ngakho-ke memezani futhi akuyilutho ukumemeza kwabangakholwa ngaphandle kokuduka nje
Ngempela thina siyazelekelela izithunywa zethu kanye nalabo abakholwayo empilweni yakulomhlaba nangosuku abayosukuma ngalo ofakazi
Ngosuku lapho lingeke libasize abangalungile izaba labo futhi okwabo yisiqalekiso futhi okwabo yindawo embi yokuhlala
Futhi ngempela samnikeza uMose ukuholwa futhi sabenza abantwana bakwa-Israyeli ukuthi babeyizindlalifa zencwadi
Ukuhola kanye nesikhumbuzo kubantu abaqondayo
Ngakho-ke bekezela, ngempela isethembiso sikaMvelinqangi siyiqiniso futhi cela intethelelo esonweni sakho futhi ugubhe indumiso yeNkosi yakho kusihlwa nasekuseni
Ngempela labo abaphikisanayo ngamavesi kaMvelinqangi ngaphandle kwegunya elafika kubona, akukho lutho ezifubeni zabo ngaphandle kokuqhenya abangeke babenako ngakho-ke funa isiphephelo kuMvelinqangi ngempela yena ungozwayo obonayo
Ngempela ukudalwa kwamazulu nomhlaba kukhulu kakhulu kunokudalwa kwabantu kepha iningi labantu alazi
Futhi ayifani impumputhe nobonayo kanye nalabo abakholwayo futhi abenza okulungile nabenza okubi, kuncane loko enikukhumbulayo
Ngempela ihora liyeza akukho ukungabaza kulona kepha iningi labantu alikholwa
Futhi iNkosi yenu yathi, “ ngimemezeni ngizoniphendula, ngempela labo abadelela ukukhonzwa kwami bayongena esihogweni bejabhisiwe”
UMvelinqangi nguyena owanenzela ubusuku ukuthi niphumule kubona nemini ukuze nibone, ngempela uMvelinqangi ugcwele umusa kubantu kepha iningi labantu alibongi
Lowo nguMvelinqangi iNkosi yenu umdali wezinto zonke, ayikho into enokukhonzwa ngaphandle kwakhe niphendukelani emumva na
Kanjalo baphendukela emumva labo ababephika amavesi kaMvelinqangi
NguMvelinqangi owanibekela umhlaba njengendawo yokuphumulakanyenamazuluabayisakhiwowayeseyanibumba nabayisimo senu esihle futhi wanabela ezintweni ezinhle, lowo nguMvelinqangi iNkosi yenu ngakho-ke ubusisekile uMvelinqangi, iNkosi yemihlaba
Ungophilayo, ayikho into enokukhonzwa ngaphandle kwakhe ngakho-ke bizani yena nibe qotho kuyena enkolweni, udumo malube kuMvelinqangi iNkosi yemihlaba
Ithi, “ngempela ngenqatshelwe ukuthi ngikhonze labo enibakhonzayo esikhundleni sikaMvelinqangi ngenkathi kufika kunina amavesi acacile avela eNkosini yami futhi ngiphoqiwe ukuthi ngizinikele eNkosini yemihlaba
Yena uyilowo owanidala ngothuli kwasekuba yingesidoda kwasekubaingehlulebeseenikhiphaniyizinganebeseniyakhula nifinyelele ekubeni semandleni enu bese niba badala, futhi phakathi kwenu kunabafayo ngaphambi (kwalokhu) futhi nifinyelele esikhathini esinqunyiwe futhi ukuze niqonde
Nguyena ophilisayo futhi obulalayo ngakho-ke uma enquma udaba kuphela uthi kulona “ yenzeka” bese kuyenzeka
Awuboni yini labo abaphikisanayo ngamavesi kaMvelinqangi ukuthi baphendukiselwa kanjani emumva
Labo abaqamba amanga ngencwadi nangalokho esakuthumela nesithunywa bayokwazi
Ngenkathi iziphika zensimbi zisezintanyeni zabo kanye namaketango abayodonswa ngawo
Emanzini abilayo bese beshiswa emlilweni
Bese kuthiwa kubona, “ kuphi lokho enanenzela ngako uMvelinqangi abahlanganyeli ekumkhonzeni
Esikhundleni sikaMvelinqangi bayothi, “banyamalele kuthina kepha sasingamemezi lutho ngaphambilini, kanjalo uMvelinqangi uyabadukisa abangakholwa
Lokho kungenxa yokuthi naniziphakamisa emhlabeni ngaphandle kweqiniso nangenxa yokuthi nanijabula
Ngenani emasangweni esihogo nihlale phakathi ingunaphakade, yimbi indawo yoku abaqholoshayo
Ngakho-ke bekezela, ngempela isethembiso sikaMvelinqangi siyiqiniso noma sikubonisa ingxenye yaloko esibathembisa kona noma siyakubulala ngakho-ke kukuthina ukubuyiselwa kwabo
Futhi ngempela sazithumela izithunywa ngaphambilini kwakho phakathi kwazo kunalezo esikutshelile ngomlando wazo futhi phakathi kwazo kunalezo esingazange sikutshele umlando wazo futhi kwakungesikona okwesithunywa ukuthi size nophawu (noma ivesi) ngaphandle kwemvume kaMvelinqangi, ngakho-ke uma kufika impoqo kaMvelinqangi kwehlulelwa ngeqiniso futhi bazolahlekelwa abalandeli bamanga
NguMvelinqangi owanenzela imfuyo ukuze nigibele kuzona nenze nezinye izidingo futhi nidle kuzona
Futhi kuzona ninenzuzo ukuze nifinyelele ngazo ezidingweni ezisezifubeni zenu futhi phezulu kwazo naphezulu kwemikhumbi niyathwalwa
Futhi uyanikhombisa izimpawu zakhe ngakho-ke yiziphi izimpawu zikaMvelinqangi eniziphikayo
Ngakube abahambi yini emhlabeni ukuze babone ukuthi sasinjani isiphetho salabo ababengaphambilini kwabo, babebaningi kunabo futhi benamadla amakhulu nangezindlela ezweni, ngakho-ke akubasizanga lokho ababekusebenzela
Ngakho-ke kwathi lapho sezifika kubona izithunywa zabo namavesi acacile bathokoza ngalokho okwakukanye nabo okolwazi kwase kuyaqiniseka kubona lokho ababenza ngako inhlekisa
Ngakho-ke kwathi lapho sebesibona isijeziso sethu bathi sikholiwe kuMvelinqangi yedwa futhi siyakuphika lokho esasenzelangakouMvelinqangiabahlanganyeliekumkhonzeni
Kepha akuzange kubasize ukukholwa kwabo kwathi lapho sebesibona isijeziso sethu, yindlela kaMvelinqangi eseyadlula ezincekwini zakhe futhi lapho balahlekelwe abangakholwa
Ha meem
Isambulo esivela konomusa onesihawu
Incwadi, enziwe acaca amavesi ayo iQur’an engesi-arabhu yabantu abaziyo
Iletha izindaba ezimnandi futhi ingumxwayisi kepha liyafulathela iningi labo ngakho-ke bona abezwa
Futhi bathi “izinhliziyo zethu zingaphansi kwezembozo kulokho osimemela kukona futhi ezindlebeni zethu kunobuthulu futhi phakathi kwethu nawe kunesisitho, ngakho-ke sebenza (ngendlela yakho) ngempela nathi siyasebenza”
Ithi, kuphela mina ngingumuntu njengani kwembuliwe kumina ukuthi uNkulunkulu wenu nguNkulunkulu oyedwa ngakho-ke yibani ngabaqondile kuyena futhi nicele intethelelo yakhe futhi usizi kwabenzela uMvelinqangi abahlanganyeli ekumkhonzeni
Labo abangayikhokhi izakaah (ingxenye yengcebo ekhokhelwa abampofu) futhi bona bengakholwelwa empilweni ezayo
Ngempela labo abakholwayo futhi abenza okulungileyo okwabo ngumvuzo ongapheliyo
Ithi “ngukube ngempela nina anikholwa kulowo owadala umhlaba ezinsukwini ezimbili na? Futhi nimbekela izimbangi, lowo yiNkosi yemihlaba”
Futhi yabeka kuwona izintaba ngaphezulu kwawo futhi yawubusisa futhi kuwona yenza ukudla (kwezihlali) zawo ezinsukwini ezine (ukuze bazi) labo ababuzayo
Yabe seyiphendukela ezulwini lona laliyintuthu yabeseyithi kulona nasemhlabeni “wozani nobabili nithanda noma ningathandi” kokubili kwathi, “siyeza sithanda”
(INkosi yemihlaba) yabe seyikuqeda ukukwakha kwaba ngamazulu ayisikhombisa ezinsukwini ezimbili futhi yembula kulelo nalelozulu udaba lwalo futhi sahlobisa izulu elingezansi ngezibani kanye nokulondolozeka, leso yisimiso sophakeme ngamandla, isazi
Ngakho-ke uma befulathela ithi “nginexwayisile ngesehlakalo esifana nesehlakalo sika-A’D noThamud
Ngenkathi zifika kubona izithunywa ziqhamuka ngaphambili kwabo nangemumva kwabo zathi “ningakhonzi lutho ngaphandle kukaMvelinqangi” bathi, “ukube iNkosi yethu yayithanda yayizokwehlisela phansi izingelosi, ngakho-ke thina singabangakholelwa kulokho enithunywe kona”
Mayelana noA’D, babezikhukhumeza emhlabeni ngokungesilona iqiniso futhi bathi,“ngubani onamandla amakhulu ukwedlula thina?, Ababoni yini ukuthi nguMvelinqangi owabadala, yena unamandla amakhulu ngaphezulu kwabo futhi babewaphika amavesi ethu
Ngakho-ke sathumela kubona umoya onamandla ezinsukwini zeshwa ukuze sibazwise isijeziso esiyihlazo empilweni yakulomhlaba futhi isijeziso sempilo ezayo siyihlazo kakhulu futhi bona angeke balekelelwe
Futhi mayelana (nabantu) ba-Thamud sabahola, kepha bathanda ubumpumputhe kunokuholwa, ngakho-ke sabathatha isehlakalo sesijeziso esiyihlazo ngenxa yaloko ababekwenza
Futhi sabasindisa labo ababekholwa futhi abagwema ububi
Futhi khumbula ngosuku lapho ziyobe ziqoqelwa emlilweni izitha zikaMvelinqangi ziyoqhutshelwa phambili
Kuze kube yilapho uma zifika kusona ukuzwa kwazo (amadlebe azo) namehlo azo kanye nezikhumba zazo ziyofakaza maqondana nazo mayelana naloko ababekwenza
Futhi (izitha zikaMvelinqangi) ziyothi ezikhumbeni zazo, “kungani nifakaza ngathi na? izindlebe zazo namehlo azo kanye nezikhumba zazo ziyothi, “nguMvelinqangi osenze ukuthi sikhulume lowo okunguyena owenza zonke izinto ukuthi zikhulume futhi yena wanidala ekuqaleni futhi niyobuyiselwa kuyena
Futhi naningawambozi hleze amadlebe enu namehlo enu kanye nezikhumba zenu kufakaze maqondana nani, kepha nanicabanga ukuthi uMvelinqangi wayengazi kakhulu ngaloko enanikwenza
Futhi lokho ngumcabango wenu lowo enaniwucabanga ngeNkosi yenu yanibhubhisa ngakho-ke nabangabanye babalahlekelwe
Ngakho-ke uma bebekezela umlilo yindawo yabo yokuhlala futhi uma befuna ukuthokozisa (uMvelinqangi) ngakho-ke bona abayibona balabo abavunyelwe ukuthokozisa
Futhi sababela abangane abakhulu, abenza kwabukeka kukuhle kubona lokho okwakungaphambili kwabo kanye nalokho okwakungemumva kwabo futhi yaqiniseka kubona inkulumo njengoba yaqiniseka ezizweni esezadlula ngaphambilini kwabo (izizwe) zamajinn kanye nabantu, ngempela bona babelahlekelwe
Futhi labo abangakholwanga bathi, “ningayilaleli leQur’an futhi nenze umsindo uma ifundwa ukuze ninqobe”
Ngakho-ke ngempela siyobazwisa labo abangakholwanga isijeziso esinzima futhi ngempela siyobanika umvuzo wokubi kakhulu lokho ababekwenza
Lowo ngumvuzo wezitha zikaMvelinqangi – umlilo, okwabo lapho phakathi kuyoba yikhaya langunaphakade (lokhu) yinkokhelo ngenxa yokuthi babephika amavesi ethu
Futhi	labo	ababengakholwa	bayothi,	“Nkosi	yethu sikhombise labo abasidukisa abangama-jinn nabantu ukuze bobabili sibabeke ngaphansi kwezinyawo zethu ukuze babengaphansi kunabobonke”
Ngempela labo abathi, “iNkosi yethu nguMvelinqangi” bese beyaqonda zehlele kubona Izingelosi, ningesabi futhi ningaphatheki kabi kepha yemukelani izindaba ezimnandi zesivande enanethenjiswe sona
Thina singabangane benu empilweni yalomhlaba kanye nakwezayo futhi okwenu lapho phakathi (esivandeni) yinoma ngabe yini imiphefumulo yenu ekufisayo futhi okwenu phakathi kusona yinoma ngabe yintoni eniyifunayo
Injabulo evela kothethelelayo onesihawu
Futhi ngubani ongcono kakhulu enkulumweni kunalowo omemela kuMvelinqangi futhi enze okulungileyo futhi athi, ngempela mina ngingomunye wabazithobile ngaphansi kwentando kaMvelinqangi
Futhi akufani okuhle nokubi, vimba ngaloko okuhle kakhulu kulapho lowo ophakathi kwakho naye kunobutha kube sengathi yena ungumngane osondele
Futhi akekho oyonikwa kona (okuhle) ngaphandle kwalabo ababekezelayo futhi akekho oyonikwa kona ngaphandle komnikazi wenhlanhla enkulu
Futhi uma usathane ekuchezukisa ngakho-ke funa isiphephelo kuMvelinqangi ngempela yena ungozwayo owaziyo
Futhi ezinye zezimpawu zakhe ubusuku nemini nelanga nenyanga ningaliguqeli ilanga nenyanga kepha guqelani uMvelinqangi okunguyena owadala kona uma kungukuthi nguyena enimkhonzayo
Kepha uma bezikhukhumeza ngakho-ke labo abaseNkosini yabo bayayidumisa ubusuku nemini futhi bona abakhathali
Futhi ezinye zezimpawu zakhe ukuthi ubona umhlaba awutheli lutho kwaba yilapho sehlisela phezulu kwawo amanzi uyanyakaza futhi ukhukhumale, ngempela lowo owuphilisayo ungumphilisi wokufile ngempela yena wenza zonke izinto
Ngempela labo abaphendukezela amavesi ethu abafihlekile kuthina, ngakube lowo ophonswa emlilweni ungcono noma uza ephephilengosuku lokuvuka kwabafileyo yenzani lokho enikufisayo ngempela yena (uMvelinqangi) ubona konke enikwenzayo
Ngempela labo abangakholelwanga esikhumbuzweni kulapho sesifikile kubona futhi ngempela sona siyincwadi ephakeme ngezinga
Amanga akezi kuyona ngaphambili kwayo nangemumva kwayo isambulo esivela konobuhlakani odunyiswayo
Akukho lutho olushiwoyo kuwena ngaphandle kwaloko okwashiwo esithunyweni ngaphambilini kwakho, ngempela iNkosi yakho ngumnikazi wentethelelo futhi ngumnikazi wesijeziso esibuhlungu
Futhi ukube besiyenzile iQur’an ngolimi lakwelinye izwe ngempela babezokuthi, “ kungani ingachazwanga imininingwane yamavesi ayo? Kungani hhayi ngesi-Arabhu kanye nom’Arabhu?” ithi yona eyalabo abakholwayo, umholi kanye nomelaphi futhi labo abangakholwa ezindlebeni zabo kunobuthuli futhi bona (ubuthuli) kuwubumpumputhe kubona, labo-ke babizwa endaweni ekude
Futhi ngempela samnikeza uMose incwadi kwase kuvela impikiswano kuyo futhi ukube kwakungesingenxa yegama elaselidlulile elivela eNkosini yakho, ngempela kwakuzokwehlulelwa phakathi kwabo futhi ngempela bona basekungabazeni okukhulu ngayo
Noma ngabe ngubani owenza okulungileyo ngakho-ke kungokomphefumulo wakhe futhi noma ngabe ngubani owenza okubi ngakho-ke kuphambene naye futhi iNkosi yakho ayinako ukungabi nobulungiswa ezincekwini
Luqondene naye ulwazi lwehora futhi asikho isithelo esiphumayo ekhasini laso futhi akekho owesifazane okhulelwayo noma azale ngaphandle kolwazi lwakhe futhi ngosuku lapho ebabiza (ethi) “baphi abahlanganyeli bami bayothi, “ siyamemezela kuwena ukuthi akekho phakathi kwethu ufakazi”
Futhi kuyonyamalala kubona lokho ababekubiza ngaphambilini futhi bayocabanga ukuthi abanayo indawo yokukhosela
Umuntu akakhathali ukucela okuhle kepha uma ethintwa okubi uphatheka kabi aphelelwe yithemba
Futhi uma simzwisa umusa ovela kuthina emva kokuba ukuhlupheka sekumthintile ngempela uthi, “lokhu kungokwami futhi angicabangi ukuthi ihora liyofika futhi uma ngiphindiselwe
eNkosini yami ngempela okwami okuhle kakhulu kuyona, ngakho-ke ngempela siyobatshela labo abangakholwanga ngalokho ababekwenza futhi ngempela siyobazwisa isijeziso esinzima
Futhi uma sikhombisa umusa kumuntu uyahoxa futhi afulathele kepha uma ethintwa okubi wenza umthandazo omude
Ithi, “ngakube nibonile yini uma ivela kuMvelinqangi (iQur’an) nabeseniyayiphika, ngakube ngubani oduke kakhulu kunalowo osekuhlubukeni okukude le!”
Siyobakhombisa izimpawu zethu emhlabeni kanye nasemiphefumulweni yabo kuze kube sobala kubona ukuthi yona iyiqiniso, ngakube akwanele yini ukuthi iNkosi yakho yona ingufakazi phezulu kwezinto zonke? 55. Ain Sin Qaf
Kanjalo uyakwembula kuwena kanye nakulaba ababengaphambilini kwakho, nguMvelinqangi ophakeme ngamandla onobuhlakani
Kungokwakhe noma ngabe yini esemazulwini kanye noma ngabe yini esemhlabeni futhi yena uphakeme kakhulu, mkhulu
Amazulu angase adabuke phakathi ngaphezulu kwawo futhi izingelosi zigubha indumiso yeNkosi yazo futhi zicelela labo abasemhlabeni intethelelo bheka! Ngempela uMvelinqangi yena ungothethelelayo onesihawu
Futhi labo abathatha (abanye) abavikeli esikhundleni sakhe, uMvelinqangi ungumlondolozi phezulu kwabo futhi wena awusiyena umphathi phezulu kwabo
Futhi kanjalo siyembulile kuwena iQur’an ngesi-Arabhu ukuze uxwayise unina wamadolobha kanye noma ngabe ngobani abawazungelezile futhi uxwayise ngosuku lokuhlangana, akukho ukungabaza ngalo, ingxenye iyokuba sesivandeni futhi (enye) ingxenye ibe semlilweni ovuthayo
Futhi ukube uMvelinqangi wayethanda wayezobenza isizwe esisodwa kepha ufaka lowo amthandayo emseni wakhe futhi izoni azinaye umvikeli noma umsizi
Noma ngakube bazithathela abavikeli esikhundleni sakhe, kepha nguMvelinqangi ongumvikeli futhi yena uphilisa abafile futhi yena wenza zonke izinto
Futhi noma ngabe yini eniphikisana kuyona, ngakho-ke isehlulelo sayo sikuMvelinqangi, lowo nguMvelinqangi iNkosi yami ngethembele kuyena futhi ngiphendukela kuyona ngokuzisola
Umdali wamazulu nomhlaba wanenzela phakathi kwenu ngakubili futhi nasezinkomeni ngakubili, uyaniphindaphinda akukho lutho olufana naye futhi yena ungozwayo obonayo
Ngezakhe izihluthulelo zamazulu nomhlaba. Uyaselula isabelo kunoma ngabe ngubani amthandayo futhi anciphise, ngempela yena uyisazi sazo zonke izinto
UMvelinqangi wanibekela inkolo leyo ayibekela uNowa kanye naleyo esiyembulile kuwena kanye nesayembula ku- Abrahamu nakuMose kanye nakuJesu ukuthi baqinise inkolo, futhi ningaqembukelani kuyona, kunzima kulabo abakhonza izithombe lokho enibamemela kukona, uMvelinqangi uziqokela lowo amthandayo futhi uholela kuyena lowo ophendukela kuyena ngokuzisola
Futhi babengaqembukelene kwaze kwaba yingaphambili kokuba sebefikelwe ulwazi ngenxa yomona nenzondo phakathi kwabo futhi ukube kwakungesingenxa yegama eselidlulile elivela eNkosini yakho esikhathini esimisiwe kwakuzokwehlulelwa phakathi kwabo, futhi ngempela labo ababenziwe ukuthi badle ifa lencwadi emva kwabo ngempela basekungabazeni okunzima ngayo
Ngakho-ke kulokho mema futhi ume uqine njengokuba uphoqiwe futhi ungalandeli izifiso zabo futhi ithi, “ngikholiwe kulokho okwembulwa nguMvelinqangi okuyincwadi futhi ngiphoqiwe ukuthi ngenze ubulungiswa phakathi kwenu, uMvelinqangi yiNkosi yethu neNkosi yenu, okwethu yimisebenzi yethu nokwenu yimisebenzi yenu, ayikho impikiswanophakathikwethunani, uMvelinqangiuyosiqoqela ndawonye futhi kukuyena ukuphindela kokugcina
Futhi labo abaphikisanayo ngoMvelinqangi emva kokuba sekwamukeliwe impikiswano yabo iyize leze eNkosini yabo futhi phezulu kwabo kunentukuthelo (kaMvelinqangi) futhi okwabo yisijeziso esinzima
NguMvelinqangi owembula incwadi ngeqiniso nangesikalo, futhi yini ekwenza wazi ukuthi mhlawumbe ihora selisondele
Ukulisheshisa (ihora bayakufisa) labo abangakholelwa kulona kulapho labo abakholwayo belesaba futhi bayazi ukuthi lona liyiqiniso bheka! Ngempela labo abaphikisanayo mayelana nehora ngempela basekudukeni okukude le
UMvelinqangi unomusa ezincekwini zakhe wabela noma ngabe ngubani amthandayo futhi yena uqatha, ungophakeme ngamandla
Noma ngabe ngubani ofisa isivuno sempilo ezayo siyamunezelela esivunweni sakhe futhi noma ngabe ngubani ofisa isivuno salomhlaba simunika sona futhi empilweni ezayo angeke abenayo ingxenye
Noma ngakube banabahlanganyeli ababamisele inkolo, lokho angakuvumelanga uMvelinqangi futhi ukube kwakungesingenxa yegama lamanqamu ngempela kwakuzokwehlulelwa phakathi kwabo futhi ngempela izoni okwazo yisijeziso esibuhlungu
Uyozibona izoni zesaba ngenxa yezakusebenzela futhi kona kwehlela kubona futhi labo abakholwayo futhi abenza okulungileyo bayokuba sezimfundeni zezivande, okwabo kuyoba yinoma ngabe yini abayifunayo ngaphambili kweNkosi yabo, lowo ngumusa omkhulu
Lokho, yilokho uMvelinqangi akutshela izinceku zakhe njengezindaba ezinhle lezo ezakholwa futhi ezenza okulungileyo, ithi, “angiwuceli umvuzo kunina ngakho ngaphandle kothando ezihlotsheni zami nakunoma ngabe ngubani osebenzela okuhle siyomunezelela kukona okuhle, ngempela uMvelinqangi ungothethelelayo obongayo
Noma bathi, “uqambela uMvelinqangi amanga ngakho-ke uma uMvelinqangi ethanda uyayisicilela inhliziyo yakho, futhi uMvelinqangi uyawasusa amanga aqinisekise iqiniso ngamazwi akhe, ngempela yena uyisazi salokho okusezifubeni
Futhi nguyena owamukela ukuphenduka ezincekwini zakhe futhi othethelela izenzo ezimbi futhi (uMvelinqangi) uyakwazi lokho enikwenzayo
Futhi uyabaphendula labo abakholwayo futhi abenza izenzo ezilungileyo futhi abanezelele emseni wakhe, futhi abangakholwa okwabo yisijeziso esinzima
Futhi ukube uMvelinqangi wayeselulile isabelo sezinceku zakhe ngempela zazizohlubuka emhlabeni, kepha usehlisa ngendlela athanda ngayo ngempela yena ngezinceku zakhe uyazi uyabona
Futhi nguyena owehlisela phansi imvula emuva kokuba bephelelwe yithemba futhi awusabalalise umusa wakhe futhi yena ungumvikeli ofanele ukudunyiswa
Futhi ezinye zezimpawu zakhe yindalo yamazulu nomhlaba kanye nakho konke akusakaza kukona kokubili (amazulu nomhlaba) okuyizidalwa ezinyakazayo futhi yena unawo amandla okubaqoqela ndawonye uma ethanda
Futhi noma ngabe yiliphi ishwa elinivelelayo kungenxa yalokho izandla zenu ezikusebenzele futhi (uMvelinqangi) uyathethelela kakhulu
Futhi nina aniyibona abaphunyukayo emhlabeni futhi aninaye umvikeli nomelekeleli ngaphandle kukaMvelinqangi
Futhi ezimpawini zakhe imikhumbi olwandle, okusengathi yizintaba
Uma ethanda uyawuthulisa umoya, bese (ulwandle) lunganyakazi endaweni yalo yangaphezulu, ngempela kulokho kunezimpawu kulowo nalowo obekezelayo, obongayo
Noma ababhubhise ngenxa yalokho abakusebenzela, futhi uyathethelela kakhulu
Futhi bayazi labo abaphikisanayo ngamavesi ethu (ukuthi) abanayo indawo yokuphephela
Ngakho-ke noma ngabe yini eninikwe yona yinjabulo yempilo yalomhlaba futhi lokho okukuMvelinqangi kungcono futhi kuyahlala kulabo abakholwayo futhi abathembela eNkosini yabo
Kanye nalabo abagwema izono ezinkulu nokukhohlakala futhi okuthi uma bethukuthele bathethelele
Nalabo abaphendulayo eNkosini yabo futhi abenza umthandazo futhi abenza udaba lwabo (lunqunywe) yisigungu phakathi kwabo futhi abasebenzisa kulokho esababela kona
Nalabo okuthi uma behlelwa yingcindezelo baziphindiselele
Futhi umvuzo wokubi okubi okufana nako, ngakho-ke noma ngabe ngubani othethelelayo futhi alungise umvuzo wakhe ukuMvelinqangi, ngempela yena akazithandi izoni
Futhi ngempela noma ngabe ngubani oziphindiselayo emva kokuba ecindezelwe ngakho-ke labo abanayo indlela (yokusolwa)
Kuphela indlela (yokusolwa) ikulabo abenza okungenabo ubulungiswa kubantu, futhi abacindezelayo emhlabeni ngokungesilona iqiniso, labo-ke okwabo yisijeziso esibuhlungu
Futhi ngempela noma ngabe ngubani obekezelayo futhi athethelele ngempela lokho kuwukulungisa izindaba
Futhi lowo oshiywa nguMvelinqangi ekudukeni, ngakho-ke akanaye umvikeli emva kwakhe futhi uyobona izoni okuyothi uma sezibona isijeziso zithi, “ngakube ikhona yini indlela yokuphindela?”
Futhi uyobona belethwa ngaphambili kwaso bethotshiswe yinjabhiso bebheka ngokujeqeza okufifiyelayo, futhi labo abakholwayo bayothi, “ngempela abalahlekelwe yilabo abalahlekelwa yimiphefumulo yabo kanye nemindeni yabo ngosuku lokuvuka kwabafileyo, bheka ngempela izoni zisesijezisweni esingapheliyo.”
Futhi angeke babenabo abavikeli abayobalekelela ngaphandle kukaMvelinqangi futhi noma ngabe ngubani uMvelinqangi amshiya ekudukeni akanayo indlela
Phendulani iNkosi yenu ngaphambi kokuba kufike usuku olungeke lugwenywe oluvela kuMvelinqangi, angeke nibe nesiphephelo ngalolosuku futhi angeke niphike
Kepha uma befulathela, ngakho-ke asikuthumelanga kubona njengomlondolozi, awukho (umthwalo) ophezulu kwakho ngaphandle kokudlulisela (umyalezo) futhi ngempela uma sizwisa umuntu umusa ovela kuthina uyawuthokozela futhi uma behlelwa okubi ngenxa yalokho izandla zabo ezikulethe ngaphambili, ngakho-ke umuntu akabongi
UngokaMvelinqangi umbuso wamazulu nomhlaba, udala noma ngabe yini ayithandayo, unikeza lowo amthandayo (ingane) yesifazane futhi unikeza lowo amthandayo (ingane) yesilisa
Noma abanike kokubili isilisa nesifazane futhi wenza inyumba noma ngabe ngubani amthandayo ngempela yena ungowaziyo owenza (izinto zonke)
Futhi akusikona okomuntu ukuthi uMvelinqangi akhulume naye ngaphandle kwesambulo noma ngemumva kwesembozo noma athumele isithunywa ukuze sembule ngentando yakhe noma ngabe yini ayithandayo, ngempela yena uphakeme unobuhlakani
Futhi kanjalo sasembula kuwena isambulo ngempoqo yethu, wawungazi ukuthi yini incwadi noma inkolo, kepha sayenza yaba ukukhanya esihola ngako noma ngabe ngubani esimthandayo ezincekwini zethu futhi ngempela wena uholela endleleni eqondile
Indlela kaMvelinqangi okunguyena okungokwakhe konke okusemazulwini nakho konke okusemhlabeni, ngempela ikuMvelinqangi lapho izindaba ziyoya khona ekugcineni

Ngencwadi ecacile
Ngempela siyenze yaba iQur’an engesi-Arabhu ukuze niqonde
Futhi ngempela yona ikumama wencwadi okuthina ophakeme onobuhlakani
Ngakube sizosusa isikhumbuzo kunina ngoba ningabantu abamoshayo
Futhi bangaki abaphrofethi esabathumela emandulo
Futhi kwakungakaze kufike kubona umphrofethi ngaphandle kokuthi babemenza inhlekisa
Ngakho-ke sababhubhisa labo ababeqatha kunabo ngamandla futhi sesadlula isibonelo sabasendulo
Futhi uma ubabuza ukuthi ngubani owadala amazulu nomhlaba ngempela bangathi, “owawadala ophakeme ngamandla owaziyo”
Okunguyena owanenzela umhlaba waba yindawo yokuphumula futhi wanenzela kuwona izindlela ukuze niholeke
Futhi okunguyena owehlisela phansi amanzi avela esibhakabhakeni ngesilinganiso wayesevusa ngawo izwe elifile, niyovuswa kanjalo
Futhi okunguyena owadala zonke izinto ngambili futhi wanenzela imikhumbi kanye nezinkomo lezo enizigibelayo
Ukuze nigibele emihlane yazo bese nikhumbula umusa weNkosi yenu uma senigibele phezulu kwazo bese nithi, “udumo malube kulowo osenzele lokhu futhi thina besingeke sibenako”
Futhi ngempela eNkosini yethu siyophindela
Futhi bambekela ingxenye ezincekwini zakhe, ngempela umuntu akabongi ngokucacile
Noma ngakube wazithathela kulokho akudalayo amadodakazi wayesenikhethela amadodana na
Futhi uma oyedwa wabo etshelwa ngezindaba zalokho akwenzile okuyisibonelo konomusa, ubuso bakhe bubamnyama futhi agcwale usizi
Lowo okhuliswe ngemihlobiso kulapho yena esempikiswaneni engacacile
Futhi benza izingelosi isifazane lezo okuyizona eziyizinceku zonomusa, ngakube bakubona ukudalwa kwazo na
Futhi bathi, “ukube wayethanda onomusa sasingeke sibakhonze”, abanalo ulwazi lwaloko (abenzi) lutho ngaphandle kokuqamba amanga
Noma sabanikeza incwadi ngaphambilini kwayo bona ababambelele kuyona
Kepha bathi, “ngempela thina safumana obaba bethu besendleleni futhi ngempela thina siholeleka ezinyathelweni zabo”
Futhi kanjalo asizange ngaphambilini kwakho sithumele edolobheni (ebantwini) umxwayisi ngaphandle kokuthi abanothile balo bathi, “ngempela thina safumana obaba bethu besendleleni futhi ngempela nathi silandela ezinyathelweni zabo”
Wathi “yize noma nginilethele ukuholwa okungcono kunalokho enabafumana kukona obaba benu? Bathi, “ngempela thina asikholelwa kulokho othunywe nako”
Ngakho-ke saziphindisela kubona, bheka ukuthi sasinjani isiphetho sabaphikayo
Futhi khumbula ngenkathi u-Abrahamu ethi kuyise nakubantu bakubo, “Angihlangene nalokho enikukhonzayo
Ngaphandle kwalowo owangidala futhi ngempela uzongihola
Futhi wakwenza kwaba yigama eliseleyo ezizukulwaneni ukuze ziphenduke
Kepha, ngabanika injabulo laba kanye naboyise kwaze kwaba yilapho befikelwa yiqiniso kanye nesithunywa esicacile
Futhi kwathi lapho sebefikelwa yiqiniso bathi, “leli yilumbo futhi ngempela thina asikholelwa kulona”
Futhi bathi, “kungani ingembulwanga leQur’an emadodeni amakhulu amadolobha amakhulu
Ngakube bona bayawuhlukanisa umusa weNkosi yakho, yithina esehlukanisayo phakathi kwabo ekuphileni kwabo empilweni yakulomhlaba futhi sabaphakamisa abanye babo ngaphezulu kwabanye ngamazinga ukuze abanye babo basebenzele abanye futhi umusa weNkosi yakho ungcono kunalokho abakuqoqela ndawonye
Futhi ukube abantu babengesisona isizwe esisodwa, ngempela sasizobenzela labo abangakholwa konomusa uphahla lwesiliva ezindlini zabo kanye nezitebhisi abanyuka ngazo
Futhi okwezindlu zabo yiminyango kanye nemibhede abaphumula phezulu kwayo
Nomhlobiso wegolide, futhi konke lokho kuyinjabulo yempilo yalomhlaba futhi impilo ezayo eNkosini yakho ngeyabagwema okubi
Futhi noma ngabe ngubani ofulathela isikhumbuzo sonomusa simvulela usathane ukuthi abe ngumngane wakhe
Futhi ngempela bona (osathane) bayabavimbela endleleni futhi bacabanga ukuthi bona bangabaholiwe
Kuze kube yilapho efika kuthina athi, “ukube nje phakathi kwami nawe bekunebanga lezimpumalanga ezimbili, ububi umngane omubi
Futhi angeke kunisize namhlanje njengoba nenza okungenabo ubulungiswa ukuthi nina niyahlukaniselana esijezisweni
Ngakube wena ungazenza yini izithuli ukuthi zizwe noma uhole izimpumputhe kanye noma ngabe ngubani osekudukeni okucacile
Noma ngabe siyakuthatha, ngempela thina siyoziphindisela kubona
Noma sikukhombise lokho esabakhombisa kona, ngakho-ke ngempela sinamandla phezulu kwabo
Ngakho-ke bambelela kulokho okwambuliwe kuwena, ngempela wena usendleleni eqondile
Futhi ngempela yona iyisikhumbuzo kuwena nakubantu bakho futhi niyobuzwa
Futhi buza noma ngabe ngobani esabathumela ngaphambilini kwakho abayizithunywa zethu, ngakube ngaphandle konomusa sibenzele yini izithixo ukuba bazikhonze
Futhi ngempela samuthumela uMose namavesi ethu kuFaro kanye nakubabusi bakhe, ngakho-ke wathi, “ngempela mina ngiyisithunywa seNkosi yemihlaba”
Kepha kwathi lapho esefika kubona nezimpawu zethu kwaba yilapho bezihleka
Futhi asizange sibakhombise uphawu ngaphandle kokuba lubelukhulu kunolukanye nalo, futhi sabathatha ngesijeziso ukuze mhlawumbe babuye
Futhi bathi, “Oh mlumbi! Sibizele iNkosi yakho ngalokho eyenza isethembiso ngako nawe, ngempela thina sizokuba ngabaholiwe”
Ngakho-ke kwathi lapho sesisisusile kubona isijeziso kwaba yilapho bona besephula (isethembiso)
Futhi uFaro wamemeza phakathi kwabantu bakhe wathi “O Bantu bami! Abusibona yini na obami ubukhosi base- Gibhithe? Kanye nalemifula egeleza ngaphansi kwami, ngakube aniboni yini
Ngakube angingcono yini kunalowo odelelekile (uMose) futhi akakwazi ukukhuluma ngokucacile
Ngakho-ke kungani engabekwanga phezulu kwakhe amasongo egolide noma izingelosi zize kanye naye
Ngakho-ke uFaro wabakhohlisa abantu bakhe base beyamhlonipha, ngempela bona babengabantu abephula umthetho
Ngakho-ke kwathi lapho besithukuthelisa saziphindisela kubona sabaminzisa bonke
Futhi sabenza asebedlulile kanye nesibonelo kwabeza ngemumva
FuthikwathilaphoindodanakaMariyayenziwanjengesibonelo kwaba yilapho abantu bakho bebanga umsindo ngayo (ngayo)
Futhi bathi, “ngakube onkulunkulu bethu abangcono noma uyena” abakwenzi lokho njengesibonelo ngaphandle kwempikiswano, kepha bona bangabantu abathanda ukuxabana
Akayilutho ngaphandle kokuba yinceku esabeka umusa phezulu kwayo futhi samenza wabayisibonelo ebantwini bakwa-Israyeli
Futhi ukube sasithanda sasizokwenza izingelosi phakathi kwenu emhlabeni zibe ngezilandelayo
Futhi ngempela yena uwuphawu lwehora ngakho-ke ungangabazi ngalo futhi landelani mina, lena yindlela eqondile
Futhi usathane anganivimbeli, ngempela yena uyisitha senu esigqamile
Futhi khumbula ngenkathi uJesu efika namavesi acacile wathi, “ngize kunina nobuhlakani nokuthi nginicacisele okunye kwalokho eniphikisana kukona ngakho-ke yesabani uMvelinqangi futhi ningihloniphe
Ngempela uMvelinqangi yena uyiNkosi yami neNkosi yenu ngakho-ke mkhonzeni, lena yindlela eqondile
Kepha amaqembu phakathi kwabo ayephikisana, Oh usizi! Kulabo ababenza okungenabo ubulungiswa, esijezisweni sosuku lokugcina
Ngakube balindele ngaphandle kwehora ukuthi lifike kubona masinyane kulapho bona bengaboni
Abangane ngalolosuku abanye babo bayokuba yizitha zabanye ngaphandle kwabagwema ukubi
Oh zinceku zami! Alukho uvalo kunina namhlanje futhi nina angeke nibe wusizi
Labo abakholwayo emavesini ethu futhi abazithoba ngaphansi kwentando kaMvelinqangi
Ngenani esivandeni nina namakhosikazi enu nithokoze
Kuzungeleziswe kubona izingqoko (amathileyi) egolide nezinkomishi futhi phakathi kuzona kunalokho okufiswa yimiphefumulo nokuthokozisa amehlo futhi nina lapho phakathi niyohlala ingunaphakade
Lesi yisivande enenziwe ukuthi nisidle njengefa ngenxa yalokho enanikwenza
Okwethu lapho phakathi yizithelo eziningi enidla kuzona
Ngempela izoni zisesijezisweni sesihogo ingunaphakade
Angeke bancishiselwe sona (isijeziso) futhi bona lapho phakathi bayophelelwa yithemba
Futhi asizange senze okungenabo ubulungiswa kubona kepha, bona babengabenzi bokungenabo ubulungiswa
Futhi bayokhala, “Oh malik! yenza ukuthi iNkosi yakho isiqedele (isibulale) lokhu uyothi (umalik) ngempela nina nizohlala (lapha)
Ngempela sinifikele neqiniso kepha iningi lenu liyalizonda iqiniso
Noma ngakube balenzile yini icebo odabeni? Kepha yithina abenzi bamacebo
Noma bacabanga ukuthi asizizwa yini izimfihlo zabo nezingxoxo zabo zangasese, yebo! Futhi izithunywa zethu zikanye nabo ziyabhala
Ithi uma kungukuthi onomusa unendodana ngakho-ke ngingowokuqala wezikhonzi
Mayidunyiswe iNkosi yamazulu nomhlaba iNkosi yesihlalo sobukhosi, ngaphezulu kwalokho abakuchazayo
Ngakho-ke bayeke bakhulume futhi badlale kuze kube bayahlangana ngosuku lwabo lolo abathenjiswa lona
Futhi yena uyilowo Mvelinqangi emazulwini futhi onguMvelinqangi emhlabeni futhi yena unobuhlakani uyisazi
Futhi ugcwele izibusiso lowo okungowakhe umbuso wamazulu nomhlaba nakho konke okuphakathi kwako kokubili futhi lukuyena ulwazi lwehora futhi niyobuyiselwa kuyena
Futhi labo abababizayo esikhundleni sakhe abanako ukuncengela ngaphandle kwalabo abafakazela iqiniso futhi bona bazi
Futhi uma ubabuza ukuthi ngubani owabadala, ngempela bazothi “nguMvelinqangi” baphendukiselwa kanjani emumva
Futhi ukusho kwakhe, Oh Nkosi yami! Ngempela laba ngabantu abangakholwa
Ngakho suka kubo futhi uthi, "Ukuthula." Kepha bazokwazi

Ngencwadi ecacile
Ngempela	sayithumela	phansi	ebusuku	obubusisiwe, ngempela thina sasingabaxwayisi
Kubona	(ubusuku)	kunqunywe	zonke	izindaba ezonobuhlakani
Udaba oluvela kuthina, ngempela thina sasingabathumeli
Umusa ovela eNkosini yakho, ngempela yona ingezwayo eyaziyo
INkosi yamazulu nomhlaba kanye nakho konke okuphakathi kwako kokubili ukube nina beniqinisekile
Akukho okunokukhonzwa ngaphandle kwakhe (uMvelinqangi) uyaphilisa futhi uyabulala, iNkosi yenu neNkosi yobaba benu basendulo
Kepha bona basekungabazeni, bayazidlalela nje
Ngakho-ke lindela usuku lapho isibhababhaka siyoletha intuthu egqamile
Imboza abantu, lesi yisijeziso esibuhlungu
Nkosi	yethu	sisuse	kuthina	isijeziso,	ngempela singabakholwayo
Bangaba kanjani nesikhumbuzo kulapho sezafika kubona izithunywa ezicacile
Babe sebeyasifulathela (isithunywa) futhi bathi, “sifundisiwe futhi siyahlanya”
Ngempela	siyasisusa	isijeziso	kancane	ngempela	nina niyaphindela (ekoneni)
Ngosuku lapho siyobashaya ngokushaya okukhulu, ngempela thina singabaziphindiselayo
Futhi ngempela sabalinga ngaphambilini kwabo abantu baFaro, futhi safika kubona isithunywa esihloniphekile
(UMose wathi), “zikhulule zize kimina izinceku zikaMvelinqangi, ngempela mina ngiyisithunywa esihloniphekile kunina”
Futhi ningaziphakamisi ngokuphambene noMvelinqangi, ngempela mina ngize kunina negunya elicacile
Futhi ngempela ngifune isiphephelo eNkosini yami neNkosi yenu hleze ningikhande ngamatshe
Kepha uma ningangikholwa, ngakho-ke qhelelanani nami
(UMose) wabe esebiza iNkosi yakhe ukuthi laba bangabantu abayizoni
Ngakho-ke hamba nezinceku zami ebusuku ngempela nina nizolandelwa
Futhi ushiye ulwandle lucwebile ngempela bona bayimpi ezominza
Zingaki izivande nemithombo abayishiya ngemumva
Kanye namasimu nezindawo ezinhle
Nobuntofontofo (bempilo) ababethokoza kubona
Kanjalo	sabenza	abanye	abantu	babayizindlalifa	zawo (umhlaba)
Ngakho-ke izulu nomhlaba akuzange kubakhalele futhi abazange baphunyuzwe (abantu baFaro)

KuFaro, ngempela yena wayephakeme phakathi kwabakhonza izithombe
